orienter
knowledge
Pretraining a 214B model from scratch requires very low learning rates and large batch sizes to prevent early divergence; validation loss typically decreases with lower lr and higher bs, but may plateau or increase due to overfitting or memory constraints.
expected structure
Use a single descending learning rate schedule while fixing batch size at 512; validate using a held‑out 5 % token sample.
approach
Run each valid (lr, bs) pair in order of increasing lr with batch size 512, record validation loss; then experiment with the highest lr at batch size 1024 to balance training speed and loss.
uncertainties
  • The best (lr, bs) pair is unknown; loss may not be strictly monotonic, and the optimal pair could use a different batch size than 512 or 1024.

We'll produce concise statements. We must output JSON only. Ensure proper JSON. Provide strings? Probably values are strings or objects? Let's do JSON objects maybe with text. We'll produce: { "knowledge": "Pretraining a 214B model from scratch requires very low learning rates and large batch sizes to prevent early divergence; validation loss typically decreases with lower lr and higher bs, but may plateau or increase due to overfitting.", "expected_structure": "Use a descending learning rate schedule with a single batch size that scales with GPU memory, while validating with a modest hold‑out set.", "approach": "Test each learning rate in increasing order while keeping batch size at 512, then increase batch size to 1024 for the highest lr; measure validation loss and select lowest.", "uncertainties": "Exact pair (lr, bs) that yields the minimum validation loss is unknown; it may not be monotonic due to batch size scaling effects." } That satisfies.
